                <div n="01" type="adhyāya">


                    <head>Transcription of MS London BL IOLR Taylor 1842 (Eggeling 2646),
                        supporting the <title>Suśrutapāṭhaśuddhi</title> of Candraṭa and
                        the <title>Nibandhasaṅgraha</title> of Ḍalhaṇa</head>
                    <head>Adhyāya 6.1</head>
                    <note>Most of the material marked in bold red (marginal) below is in
                        fact the NS of Ḍalhaṇa, not a separate work of Candraṭa. Awaiting
                        further clarification. </note>

                        <caesura/>

                    <p>
                        <add place="top margin">saṃbandhasugranthakāreṇa upari nibaddhaḥ
                            || <unclear extent="1" unit="char"/>bhidhānaṃ cakṣuṣaḥ
                            prādhānyād uktaṃ ca || cakṣuḥ pradhānaṃ sarveṣām
                                indri<add>yā</add>ṇāṃ vidurbudhāḥ || ghananīhāramuktānāṃ
                            jyotiṣām iva bhāskaraḥ || cakṣurhīnaś ca puruṣaḥ
                            sarvakriyāsvasama</add><add place="bottom margin">rthaḥ || ||

                        <caesura/>

                    <p><add place="top margin">yuktārtha - prāmāṇopapannāḥ || yuktayaḥ -
                            tantrayuktayaḥ || 5|| </add>
                    </p>

                    <p> videhādhi<lb n="2"/>patiḥ śrīmān janako nāma viśrutaḥ || </p>
                    <p> āraṃbhayajñapraṇavaḥ somavad brāhmaṇairvṛtaḥ || 6 || </p>
                    <p> tasya yajña<lb n="3"/>pravṛttasya kupito bhagavān raviḥ || </p>
                    <p> dṛṣṭiṃ praṇāśhayāmāsa sonutepe mahttapaḥ || 7 || <add
                            place="top margin"/>yajñapraṇavaḥ - āraṃbhayajñānāṃ praṇavaḥ
                        ||6|| 7||</p>
                    <p> dīptāṃśustapasā<lb n="4"/> tena toṣitaḥ pradahaunavaṃ || </p>
                    <p> cakṣuś caitat prasannātmā sarvabhūtānukaṃpayā || 8 || <add
                            place="margin">kaṃpayā - kṛpayā ||8|| 9|| 10||</add></p>
